#
#     Here is a file of CP/M Definitions for cpmtools, libdsk, and Flashfloppy/GOTEK
#     There could be typo's, or mistakes that have been overlooked in the creation of
#     these definitions.  If you do find typo's or mistakes please leave feedback as
#     what needs to be corrected.     
#
#
#alt     SIDES specifies that first one side then the other is written/read
#              before the cylinder number is advanced.
#
#outback CYLINDERS specifies that all tracks on the first side are recorded
#              then all tracks on second side.  Tracks on side 0 are written
#              from 0 up and side 1 down to 0.
#
#outout  EAGLE same as CYLINDERS except both sides start at zero or outermost
#              track.
#
#        COLUMBIA same as CYLINDERS except tracks are sequential from side
#              0 to side 1 ie. 0 - 79 for a 40 track disk.
#
#        EVEN-ODD means side 0 contains even-numbered tracks and side 1
#              contains odd-numbered tracks. 
#
#        SKIP means skip the first Single Density Track
#

SYSTEM A1  Generic CP/M - SSSD 8" - 128 x 26

# A1  Generic CP/M - SSSD 8" - 128 x 26
diskdef a1
  seclen 128
  tracks 77
  sectrk 26
  blocksize 1024
  maxdir 64
  skew 6
  boottrk 2
  os 2.2
end

# libdsk
[a1]
description = A1  Generic CP/M - SSSD 8" - 128 x 26
cylinders = 77
heads = 1
secsize = 128
sectors = 26
secbase = 1
datarate = HD

# flashfloppy/GOTEK
[a1]
cyls = 77
heads = 1
secs = 26
interleave = 6
bps = 128
id = 1
rpm = 360
#rpm = 300
rate = 125
mode = fm
iam = no

SYSTEM A2  Generic CP/M 3.0 - SSSD 8" - 128 x 26

# A2  Generic CP/M - SSSD 8" - 128 x 26
diskdef a2
  seclen 128
  tracks 77
  sectrk 26
  blocksize 1024
  maxdir 64
  skew 6
  boottrk 3
  os 3
end

SYSTEM ABD1  A. B. Dick Magna III - DSDD 48 tpi 5.25" - 256 x 16

SYSTEM SUP3  Superbrain QD - DSDD 48 tpi 5.25" - 512 x 10

# SUP3  Superbrain QD - DSDD 48 tpi 5.25" - 512 x 10
diskdef sup3
  seclen 512
  tracks 70
  sectrk 10
  blocksize 2048
  maxdir 64
  skew 2
  boottrk 2
# data should be complemented
# libdsk doesn't do that yet
  os 2.2
end
